 nil aryan gupta bhi un chaatro main se hai jinhone kai saal tak is ummid main taiyaari kii ki unhen bhi na sirf iaiti main padhane kaa mauka mil sakegaa balki JEE mens or advanced main unki ranking bhi kaaphi upar hogi
 But Aryan suddenly faced a tough exam and became very ill during the XII board examination
 unki tabiyat itani karaab thi ki unhen aspataal main bhartee hona padaa or maths kaa paper dene ve sidhe aspataal se pariksha haul main pahunche

 jab rigelt aae to aryan ko maths main sau main sau ank mili
 But for Aryan, there was still a long period of ordeal

 apni beemaari se pareshaan aryan padhai nahin kar paa rahe the

 enditivi se baatcheet main aryan kii maa bataatin hai ki hamen laga agar oparation karavaaya to phir jeii mens dena lagbhag asambhav ho jayega

 phir unhone pijiai chandigarh ke doctors ko consalt kiya
 PGI doctors gave the green signal to postpone the operation till Mains
 par aryan ke liye takaleef kaa daur chalata rahaa
 Aryan says that his health deteriorated in the examination hall on the day of Mains and it took him 15-20 minutes to become stable and his Mains exam was not very good
 mens ke baad parivaar ne oparation karwaane kaa nirnay liya
 Aryan from NDTV says that after the operation he felt that his days of pain had passed but it proved to be his misunderstanding
 din main do baar dressing hoti thi jo jisamen unhen kaaphi dard hota tha phir dawa khaane se jhapakiyaan aatin thi

 But after the operation, the family started to make Aryan realize that now he has to prepare himself for the exam again
 baithne main mushkil aane ke baad bhi ab aryan baithne kii practice karne lage taaki kuch padhai kar saken
 When you could not sit, you read while lying down
 aryan ke teachers unhen email par practice ke liye test papers bhejte
 During this, Aryan also realized that when he sits down to solve previous years' papers, after five minutes of the beginning, he is so lost in questions that he forgets the pain

 par aryan ko achaanak hi ek kathin pariksha kaa saamana karnaa padaa or barahavin kii board pariksha ke dauraan kaaphi biimaar ho gaye

 barahavin kii board pariksha ke baad ab jipsi mens kii baari thi

 phir jab beemaari kaa pataa chalaa to doctors kaa kahana tha ki oparation hi ek maatr rasta he
